                queue 2
                egress-hsmda

                exit
            exit

                multicast-queue 13
                queue 3
                egress-hsmda
                    queue 5
                exit
            exit
        exit

            description "drop profile"
            high-slope
                start-avg 80
                max-avg 95
                max-prob 10
                no shutdown
            exit
            low-slope
                start-avg 30
                max-avg 95
                max-prob 20
                no shutdown
            exit
        exit
    exit
